### Employee Attrition Dataset
```SQL
CREATE TABLE Employee_Attrition (
    [Age] INT,
    [Attrition] NVARCHAR(3),
    [BusinessTravel] NVARCHAR(17),
    [DailyRate] INT,
    [Department] NVARCHAR(22),
    [DistanceFromHome] INT,
    [Education] INT,
    [EducationField] NVARCHAR(16),
    [EmployeeCount] INT,
    [EmployeeNumber] INT,
    [EnvironmentSatisfaction] INT,
    [Gender] NVARCHAR(6),
    [HourlyRate] INT,
    [JobInvolvement] INT,
    [JobLevel] INT,
    [JobRole] NVARCHAR(25),
    [JobSatisfaction] INT,
    [MaritalStatus] NVARCHAR(8),
    [MonthlyIncome] INT,
    [MonthlyRate] INT,
    [NumCompaniesWorked] INT,
    [Over18] NVARCHAR(1),
    [OverTime] NVARCHAR(3),
    [PercentSalaryHike] INT,
    [PerformanceRating] INT,
    [RelationshipSatisfaction] INT,
    [StandardHours] INT,
    [StockOptionLevel] INT,
    [TotalWorkingYears] INT,
    [TrainingTimesLastYear] INT,
    [WorkLifeBalance] INT,
    [YearsAtCompany] INT,
    [YearsInCurrentRole] INT,
    [YearsSinceLastPromotion] INT,
    [YearsWithCurrManager] INT
);
```
